## Opcodes

```
  0: 0x1389 [0x1E] EventEntity looks at LocalPlayer and starts talking
  1: 0x138E [0x1D] PRINT_EVENT_MESSAGE(message_id=11893*)
    → "Hey, like, are you still running around on adventures with your friend?\u007F1\u0000\u0007"
  2: 0x1391 [0x23] WAIT_FOR_DIALOG_INTERACTION
  3: 0x1392 [0x1D] PRINT_EVENT_MESSAGE(message_id=11894*)
    → "A little curiosity never killed anyone, you know?\u007F1\u0000\u0007"

```
